[RegEX]WEATHER PREFERENCE\nThis setting disables the GLOBAL forecast in favor of more realistic weather transitions. Each weather has it's own list of preferred weathers it will change into next cycle, preventing scenarios like light rain one cycle, and a blizzard the next.|天气偏好#Environment.NewLine#此设置会关闭全局天气预报，转而采用更贴近现实的天气变化方式。每一个天气拥有自己的下一雨循环天气变化倾向列表，避免出现像是一个雨循环的天气是小雨，下个循环的天气是暴风雪的现象。
[RegEX]WEATHER RANDOMNESS\nIf you are using the Weather Preference setting, you can adjust this slider to introduce some additional randomness to the forecast. Based on the percentage, a completely random weather will be selected.|随机天气#Environment.NewLine#如果您启用了天气偏好设置，你可以调整调整这个滑块来为天气预报引入一些额外的随机性。基于百分比，将会选择一个完全随机的天气。
[RegEX]WEATHER INTENSITY\nEach weather type has a minimum and maximum intensity. In dynamic mode, weather intensity will gradually progress from the minimum to the maximum as the cycle progresses, or you can set it to a fixed value.|天气强度#Environment.NewLine#每一个天气类型拥有一个最小和最大强度。在动态模式中，天气强度会随着循环进程从最小值演变到最大值，或者您可以设定一个固定值。
[RegEX]BACKGROUND COLLISION\nEach weather particle has a chance of colliding with elements in the background instead of just normal room geometry. This can look more realistic but may also result in less particles hitting the floor in taller rooms.|背景碰撞#Environment.NewLine#每个天气粒子都会有几率撞击背景中的元素而不是房间中的常规几何结构。这会让其看起来更真实，但也可能会导致在较高的房间中撞击地板的粒子减少。
[RegEX]FORECAST STYLE\nForecast's own snow style; has it's own snowflake particles and a unique end-of-cycle Blizzard. After cycle end the temperature will decrease and the wind will pick up. Your exposure to the cold is indicated by an icy border and eventually, beating drums will signal your imminent death.|天气预报类型#Environment.NewLine#天气预报自己的降雪类型，拥有专属的雪花粒子效果以及专属的循环终末的暴风雪。在循环结束之后，温度会骤降并且风会增大。你暴露在寒冷中的程度将会由冰封边框表示，最终，敲击的鼓点会预示你即将到来的死亡。

//ScarletFlowerBulb
This is the spore-releasing bulb of a mycelial root network.<LINE>My creators used to call it Monksweed, as it frustrated them to no end whenever it managed to grow inside their old temples and monasteries.<LINE>The roots can extend for miles below the surface, and are nearly impossible to remove once they infect an area.|这是某种菌丝体释放孢子的球茎。<LINE>我的创造者曾称它们为僧侣草，他们会因为发现它们在古寺和修道院中扎了根而极度沮丧。<LINE>它们的根能在地下蔓延数英里，感染了它们的区域几乎无法复原。
Some believed the spores could make you hear strange whispers, or give you visions of the past and future if you inhaled them.<LINE>I don't know how true those rumors were, but I would be extremely careful with this if I were you.|传言说这些孢子会让你听到诡异的低语声，若你吸入它们则会看见过去与未来的幻象。<LINE>我并不确定这些传言的真实性，但如果是我的话，我会小心对待它们。
//ParrySword
Oh, what a curious find, <PLAYERNAME>... This weapon was once the personal item of one of my long-departed creators.<LINE>Its purpose was for self-defence, as its curved design and superior durability enables it to absorb and deflect blows from superior opponents.|哦！多么少见的发现，<PLAYERNAME>...这把武器曾是我早已离世的创造者之一的私人物品。<LINE>初衷是为了自卫，弯曲的设计和卓越的耐用性使它可以吸收并偏转强烈打击。
You see, my creators believed that violence was the most base and unforgivable of all vices. Conflict was rare but not unheard of,<LINE>and so weapons like these were made to protect important persons from harm without comitting such harm in return.|如你所见，我的创造者坚信暴力是最为卑劣且不可饶恕的恶行。<LINE>冲突虽然少见但并不是完全不可能发生，<LINE>因此这种武器被制造出来用于保护重要人物免受伤害且不会造成反击伤害。
This one was even equipped with a primitive AI module, to prevent it from being used for evil I assume.<LINE>It must trust you, if you were able to touch it and bring it all the way here. Perhaps it considers you its new wielder, even.|这一把甚至配备了初级人工智能程序，我猜是避免武器被用于作恶。<LINE>而你能接触它并将它一路带到这里，那它一定信任着你。<LINE>甚至可能已经将你认作新主人了。
